<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1801694e-552f-4200-babf-1ef25657f663'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer4078709045661232426"><b>This is a stand alone novel that is an adult spin-off of the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/66252-lux' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lux Series</a></b> You do not need to read a Lux book to read Obsession and vice versa.<br/><br/>He’s arrogant, domineering, and...   <span id="freeText4078709045661232426" style="display:none"><b>This is a stand alone novel that is an adult spin-off of the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/66252-lux" rel="nofollow noopener">Lux Series</a></b> You do not need to read a Lux book to read Obsession and vice versa.<br /><br />He’s arrogant, domineering, and... To. Die. For.<br /><br />Hunter is a ruthless killer. And the Department of Defense has him firmly in their grasp, which usually doesn’t chafe too badly because he gets to kill bad guys. Most of the time he enjoys his job. That is, until he’s saddled with something he’s never had to do before: protect a human from his mortal enemy.<br /><br />Serena Cross didn’t believe her best friend when she claimed to have seen the son of a powerful senator turn into something... unnatural. Who would? But then she witnesses her friend’s murder at the hands of what can only be an alien, thrusting her into a world that will kill to protect their secret.<br /><br />Hunter stirs Serena’s temper and her lust despite their differences. Soon he’s doing the unthinkable—breaking the rules he’s lived by, going against the government to keep Serena safe. But are the aliens and the government the biggest threats to Serena’s life… or is it Hunter?</span>
  <a data-text-id="4078709045661232426" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText1559189992610628250" style="display:none">It’s official! They are different from the Luxens and they fight in order to protect the humans and their kind. Yet , like in every species , some arums kill just for fun.<br><br><b>Hunter</b><br><i>“That´s an alien. I´m an alien. We´re aliens. Aliens everywhere, acutally, which is why we have to leave. I´m sure someone called the police by now.”</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401061i/777822.jpg" alt=" photo 43a05e0f-c714-4874-b64e-58bc2f8e3c77_zpsd5cd3bdd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Serena</b><br><i>“Never in my life had I been more frustrated. Go figure it wouldn't be with a human but a freaking alien. At least I now knew that the male species were asses no matter what planet they hailed from.”</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793838i/583299._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Serena’s best friend had the misfortune to be dating a Luxen . An argument that she eavesdropped costs her , her life . She talks with Serena about what she saw but Serena only thinks that her friend is going nuts. Seriously , they were fighting and then turned into lighting humans ? Who would believe this story ? Apparently no one , neither our book heroine . It is known that you don’t believe something until you witness it with your own eyes . In this case it was too late .<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Serena’s friend was killed by a Luxen. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>At this point we meet Hunter .<br><br><b>Bad never felt so good</b><br><br>He is arrogant and harsh. A human’s life is not important to him but the DOD forces him to <i>babysit</i> one. Unwittingly he obeys but he never thought that this human would change his life .<br>When they meet each other for the first time I couldn’t stop grinning .<br>Hunter is one of the cockiest and most arrogant heros ever , which of course is not bad at all. He pisses her off all the time with his attitude . There are times that you will want to punch him.<br><br><i>“Are you done acting like a psychotic, cracked-out Muppet baby?" he asked, and I could tell by the way his fingers spasmed around my wrists, he really wanted to shake me. <br>"Or do you need a couple more moments to return to sanity? I have all day. And you actually feel kind of good under me, so take your time.”</i><br><br>He is unbelievable and that’s the reason I love him . Well , almost…<br>It’s hard not to fall for Mr. Six-pack heaven.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401061i/777823.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Things between them start getting more complicating. Hunter , like a typical male , cant hold himself back and with every opportunity flirts with her . Hahaha Hunter is not so much a flirting type .<br><i>
  <b>I knocked her out . Again . Aw fuck.</b>
</i><br>Even a simple kiss is dangerous for her if he doesn’t control himself . Taking control is difficult though because humans are little snacks for the Arums . He doesn’t give up though , he is willing to try again and again. <br><br>One of the best things about Hunter except from his hands *wink*<br>(What??He likes wood crafting!!) is that he is also a great cook.<br>Oh yes! Both hot and talented .<br><br><b>My brother gave me shit about it , so did Dex.<br>Fuck them I was a great cook.</b><br><br>Hunter is there to protect her but what happens when the government wants you dead?<br>When everyone wants the worst for you?<br><i>He will kill every bastard that will appear in his way in order to protect her.</i><br><br>That’s what I liked about him . He is fierce and devoted. He doesn’t give a rats a@@ when it comes to her safety .<br>The funny thing is that Serena has already admitted to herself that she <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[loves him <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> but she cant understand his motives . Why he is putting his life on danger for her .<br><b>Why are you helping me?</b><br>No one knows why , neither Hunter . It is wrong in all ways to help her . His job is over after all.<br><br><u>Why I loved Hunter</u>: OMG his arrogance knows no bounds . Sometimes I was like *giggles* “He didn’t say that , did he?”<br>He is so dangerous that in his way are only lying the dead bodies of Luxens . Serena wakes up unprecedented feelings to him .<br>Ha one of the funniest moments was when he woke up in the middle of the night and caught himself cuddling . For him it is too human-ish and shows weakness .<br><br><i>Fav quote:</i><br><b>”Your arrogance is rooted in stupidity.”<br>“And your lifespan is getting shorter by the second.”</b><br>Never , piss him. I’m serious , bad things happen when he’s pissed.<br><br><u>Why I loved Serena</u>: She is both shy and smart . I liked the fact that she accepted Hunter and who he was . She was always encouraging him to turn into his true form . It wasn’t scary for her and it meant a lot to Hunter . She is a strong girl , not a badass though. I love the fact that she managed to bring Hunter’s best behavior out.<br>When I was reading this book I thought that a good soundtrack would be<br> <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=oKBlS88duDA" rel="nofollow noopener">Etostone - Together ft. Jason McKnight</a><br><br><i>I wanna live my life with you<br>Every moment close to you<br>Never to lose my love for you<br>Finally, my wish has all come true<br>I wanna live my life with you<br>Side by side to walk on through<br>No matter what happens - I turn into<br>With every breath - I take, Together with you... <br><br>Baby it's alright , stay all night , <br>Baby it's alright , together , together tonight.<br><br>Let me take you high, Baby one more time<br>Let me take you high, and shoot up to the sky<br>Let me take you high, Baby one more time<br>Just one more time</i><br><br><br>Overall it was a great read! It is not necessary to read the lux series firstly but it would be nice if you did.<br>Thank you Georgia , Debra , Sandra and Christy for this buddy read!<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401061i/777824._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401061ra/777825.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_630161894" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/630161894" />
    <a title="Dd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9444787-dd"><img alt="Dd" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/630161894?book_show_action=true">Jun 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dd" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dd" href="/user/show/9444787-dd">Dd</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer630161894" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1816214342310863251"><br/>***ATTENTION ALL DAEMON LOVERS***<br/><br/><b>So, is it a shadow? Total darkness? Or a black hole?<br/><br/>Or is it an Arum.<br/><br/>Well, it’s....</b><br/><br/><i>“Tell me to shut up one more time and I’m going to rip out your tongue and make you eat it. Got that?”</i><br/><br/><b>....Hunter!</b><br/><br/>---------------------------------------------------------<br/><br/><i>'In the dim, almost but-not-quite seedy bar lights, I stared openmouthed at my best friend in what had to be the most unattractive manner.'</i><br/><br/>Well to be truthful what else could Serena do? Afterall her best friend Mel</span>
  <span id="freeText1816214342310863251" style="display:none"><br />***ATTENTION ALL DAEMON LOVERS***<br /><br /><b>So, is it a shadow? Total darkness? Or a black hole?<br /><br />Or is it an Arum.<br /><br />Well, it’s....</b><br /><br /><i>“Tell me to shut up one more time and I’m going to rip out your tongue and make you eat it. Got that?”</i><br /><br /><b>....Hunter!</b><br /><br />---------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><i>'In the dim, almost but-not-quite seedy bar lights, I stared openmouthed at my best friend in what had to be the most unattractive manner.'</i><br /><br />Well to be truthful what else could Serena do? Afterall her best friend Mel was claiming to have seen an alien.And that supposed alien was the Senator's son.<br /><br />Hilarious,really.<br /><br />But being a good friend, Serena asked Mel to stay with her while in her head she was spewing out possible ailments like she was doing a mental grocery list: psychotic break with reality, schizophrenia, anxiety attack with hallucinations, or a brain tumor....<br /><br />The possibilities were endless.<br /><br /><br /><b>But all that changed when she saw Mel get murdered by the very type of creature she had described.<br /><br />An alien.</b><br /><br />--------------------------------------------------------<br /><br />Okay, so all Daemon lovers, by now we know exactly who Luxens are, love them, and hate the Arums.<br /><br />Ummm...sorry Daemon, you know I still love you, but here we see a slightly different side.<br /><br /><br /><b>Hunter is of course the highest up in the food chain.<br /><br />He’s cunning, he’s ruthless, he’s cruel, he's a predator.<br /><br />Extremely powerful, he’s certainly no saviour.He’a a born and bred killer.</b><br /><br /><br /><br />But then the DOD asks him to babysit and protect a human female.<br /><br /><br /><b>A predator protecting it’s prey? What do you think will happen?</b><br /><br /><br /><i>‘Shit. I was not happy about this. There wasn’t a patient bone in my body and the only reason I was ever around a woman was to sate a primal hunger. I didn’t watch over them. I didn’t protect them. It wasn’t in my nature, and the officers knew that. I wasn’t the good guy here.<br /><br />There was a good chance I’d kill Miss Cross.’</i><br /><br /><br /><b>Oh yessss....BOOOOOOOOOOM!!!!</b><br /><br />----------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>Hunter, whatever he expected, did not really expect HER!</b><br /><br /><br /><i>“Are you insane?” he growled. “Look at me!”<br /><br />Shaking my head frantically, I kept my eyes squeezed shut. “Please don’t—”<br /><br />“Please don’t what? Strangle the ever-loving common sense into you? I might do that.” There was a pause and his chest rose against mine. <br /><br />“Jesus H. Christ, woman, I didn’t sign up for this. I think you gave me a flesh wound.”</i><br /><br /><br /><b>He's an ass.A total domineering ass.Give him an inch, he'll take miles and miles.</b><br /><br /><br /><i>“Get off me.” I tried to push him off, but that didn’t work. “Get off me now!”<br /><br />“Or what?” He tilted his head down so that his mouth was inches from mine. “You going to pick up a picture frame next and wing it at my head?”<br /><br />“Maybe,” I snapped back.<br /><br />“Then I can’t let you up.”<br /><br />I stared at him in disbelief and sputtered, “You can’t— Get off!”<br /><br />One single brow arched up. “I can’t get off? Oh, I most definitely can get off.”<br /><br />The flush increased until I felt like I was under the sweltering sun. Muscles in my stomach tightened. “That’s not what I meant and you know it.”<br /><br />“Hmm, so you say…so you say.”</i><br /><br /><br /><b>But Serena can not stop her heart from going into an overdrive whenever he's near.</b><br /><br /><br /><i>'Holy hotness...<br /><br />Jeans hung low on narrow hips. Hunter’s stomach was perfection—each taut muscle tight and totally lickable. Not that I’d ever licked a man’s stomach before, but now I got why someone would want to. I was in six-pack heaven. He even had those dips beside the hip-bones...'</i><br /><br /><br /><b>Hmmm...oh sorry!! Was busy wiping away my drool.</b><br /><br /><br /><b>Oh and by the way I can't not tell you about one of my favourite scenes, where he SPANKS her!!!!</b><br /><br /><br /><i>'With one arm secure around her waist, I gave her ass a friendly pat with my free hand. “You should really watch your language. It’s not very ladylike.”<br /><br />“Don’t you dare smack my—” A yawn cut her off, totally ruining the level of threat.“You high-handed, arrogant son of a—”<br /><br />Whamp! This smack was a little harder. “Language, Serena.”<br /><br />What came out of her mouth next almost made me drop her. She got her ass smacked again for that and after the third time, she quieted down.'</i><br /><br /><br /><b>(Daemon, I still love you baby, but you've gotta learn something from Hunter!!)</b><br /><br /><br /><i>“I want to hear you call my name when you come.” His voice was thick, smoky; his lips moving against my breast. “I want to hear you scream my name.”</i><br /><br /><br /><b>**MAJOR SWOON ATTACK!!!!**</b><br /><br />--------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>But all this doesn't change the fact that he's a predator, and she....his prey.</b><br /><br /><br />So what's holding him back? Is it the DOD pulling his strings? Is that the reason she's still alive? <br /><br /><br />Is that the reason he's her <b>protector</b> instead of the other way round?<br /><br /><br /><b>Or has Serena somehow managed to wiggle inside his whatever-organ-beats-inside-his-alien-chest?</b><br /><br /><br />And then suddenly when everything goes awry, Hunter will have to choose....and soon.Because Serena’s time is running out.<br /><br /><br />Everyone, the government, the Luxen, the Arum, everyone’s against her and wants her dead.<br /><br /><br /><b>How far will Hunter go to protect her? Read the book to find it out.</b><br /><br />--------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><br />Now, time to clarify a few things ---<br /><br /><b>1)</b> This is an Arum novel, yes.This takes place in the exact world, in the exact time period in which Daemon and Katy reside.<br /><br /><b>2)</b> The perspective, as expected, is widely different.You'll be wondering over what's right and what's wrong even after you finish this book.<br /><br /><b>3)</b> It has targeted a crowd more mature and so is, of course, more steamy than the Lux series.<br /><br /><b>4) Last but not the least, the ending won’t kill you!</b><br /><br /><br />So Readers, all that said... ENJOY this book!!!<br /><br /><br /><b>That's all for now,<br /><br />Ta-Ta!!</b><br /><br /><br /><b>P.S.:-</b> For all Daemon lovers,if you feel as if you're cheating on Daemon, or betraying him, then remember....<br /><br /><b>Hunter oozes that kind of dark sex appeal that made good girls do bad, bad things. Over and over again.</b><br /><br />....and rest your conscience.<br /><br />(At least that's what I've done.)<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

</a><br/><br/>I feel like a traitor. And it’s all because of this guy...<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/9a477cd2-3985-40e3-b2f8-33f630989b18_zps8b22d5ec.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><b>
  <i>‘And here’s another impolite thing for you. I don’t give a fuck.’</i>
</b><br/><br/>I sooooo love Daemon from the Lux series, its not even funny. SO how is it possible that I love Hunter, this Arum (the Lux’s enemy) EVEN MORE? I dunno... but I do! Hunter has an attitude and I loved it! He is also all kinds of sexy and hilarious! <br/><br/>Now to the story- Serena is just a normal 23 year old girl. She has a wacky best friend, Mel, who </span>
  <span id="freeText9846524318872979191" style="display:none"><b> 5 Fantastic Stars! </b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/992fa1a2-13e5-482d-8135-05a40ec92d49_zpseb7f01e4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420645i/834661.jpg" alt=" photo 992fa1a2-13e5-482d-8135-05a40ec92d49_zpseb7f01e4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I feel like a traitor. And it’s all because of this guy...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/9a477cd2-3985-40e3-b2f8-33f630989b18_zps8b22d5ec.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420645i/834662.jpg" alt=" photo 9a477cd2-3985-40e3-b2f8-33f630989b18_zps8b22d5ec.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>‘And here’s another impolite thing for you. I don’t give a fuck.’</i>
</b><br><br>I sooooo love Daemon from the Lux series, its not even funny. SO how is it possible that I love Hunter, this Arum (the Lux’s enemy) EVEN MORE? I dunno... but I do! Hunter has an attitude and I loved it! He is also all kinds of sexy and hilarious! <br><br>Now to the story- Serena is just a normal 23 year old girl. She has a wacky best friend, Mel, who she meets one night for drinks after work. Mel is talking crazy. She has seen something that has her freaking out. A guy she is seeing was arguing with his brother and lit himself up like a light bulb. Serena doesn’t know what to think... <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/8f398652-6cdc-45c2-98c2-a4bca8bb6286_zpsc2653835.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420646i/834663.jpg" alt=" photo 8f398652-6cdc-45c2-98c2-a4bca8bb6286_zpsc2653835.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>‘I need more wine for this shit.’</i>
</b><br><br>She decides to have Mel come over her place so they can talk more. But then Serena witnesses something crazy... her best friends car getting blown up, with Mel in it. Serena is upset, and freaked out. She gets questioned and tells the detectives everything she knows. She saw the same think Mel did. She knows she sounds crazy, but she saw what she saw. The Lux aren’t all good, we find out in this book. They can’t have Serena out there, so they want to take matters into their own hands. The D.O.D steps in and sends someone to watch over her and protect her for the time being. Hunter, an Arum- someone who can defend her against the Lux if need be.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/7f8e697e-0a7c-4166-8e1f-10ab9bb765c0_zpsdbcd3d84.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420646i/834664.jpg" alt=" photo 7f8e697e-0a7c-4166-8e1f-10ab9bb765c0_zpsdbcd3d84.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Hunter is an Arum in his late twenties/early thirties. He doesn’t really do the whole human interaction thing. He works for the DOD, but he looks out for himself. <br><b>OMG</b> Hunter and Serena’s back and forth banter had me rolling with fits of laughter. They were just hilarious together. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Are you done acting like a psychotic, cracked-out Muppet baby?" he asked, and I could tell by the way his fingers spasmed around my wrists, he really wanted to shake me. <br>"Or do you need a couple more moments to return to sanity? I have all day. And you actually feel kind of good under me, so take your time.” <br><br>“You have a feisty little attitude, don’t you?”<br> “You’re about to get a feisty little foot up your ass.”<br><br>“You’re so cocky.”<br> “Ah, don’t say anything with the word cock in it.”<br> “What? Will I wake the slumbering beast?”<br> “The slumbering beast is always awake around you.”<br><br>“Is there ever a moment when you’re not bossing someone around?”<br> “Probably not.” <br>“And do you realize how rude and annoying it is?” <br>“Yes. And before you ask, I don’t give a shit if it’s annoying and rude.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Serena doesn’t really want to be protected. She wants answers. Hunter gives her some, but he is also quite about some things. It drives Serena crazy.<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Never in my life had I been more frustrated. Go figure it wouldn't be with a human but a freaking alien. At least I now knew that the male species were asses no matter what planet they hailed from.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>The more time they spend together, the more Serena learns about Hunter and his kind. The more Hunter starts to like her. Oh my the chemistry between these two... they were sizzling hot together! And the sexual tension just kept building and building... Hunter is hot as hell! <br><b>
  <blockquote>I was still a red-blooded, twenty-three year old woman sitting in front of a man, who may not be a hundred-percent human but had to have caused a panty-dropping crisis across the universe. </blockquote>
</b><br>And when they finally got ‘together’. WOW. Double WOW. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Where were we? Oh yeah, I want to hear you scream my name.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/5c6c5559-d362-407a-8303-1e68b7824e1e_zpsbbf88a82.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420646i/834665.jpg" alt=" photo 5c6c5559-d362-407a-8303-1e68b7824e1e_zpsbbf88a82.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The two start to develop a connection, and start to have feelings for one another. Serena is funny, feisty and stubborn, but Hunter finds himself liking those things about her. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Damn, you have a mouth on you. I like it.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> Hunter was a jerk at first. But a hot jerk. A funny jerk. The BEST kind of jerk! I loved him!!!!!<br><br>Things don’t stay smooth for long. It seems all kinds of people are after Serena now, and Hunter has to chose... Does he protect her and help her, even though she is just a human and it could put his life at risk, or does he just let whatever happen to her and not worry about it... he is an Arum after all. What do you think?<br><br><br>If you enjoyed the Lux series, chances are you will enjoy this one too. This book is considered a stand alone, but personally, I wouldn’t read it unless you’ve read the Lux series. To me it was just as good, maybe even a little better (although that my have something to do with the steam factor going up BIG TIME). Be prepared to seriously <b>laugh your ass off</b> and <b>fall in love</b> with <u>HUNTER!</u></span>

<div id="review_533387227" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/533387227" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/533387227?book_show_action=true">Feb 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=super-cheese">super-cheese</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=frustrating">frustrating</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=aliens">aliens</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer533387227" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8891234139315731856">I am so sorry. I am SO sorry. <b>I am sooooo sorry.</b><br/><br/>It's not often when I write a review and worry about having a difference of opinion from my friends - because if I had to worry, I'd have to do it for every single book review with the varied group of friends I have. Thankfully, I have awesome friends who don't mind me most of the time. However...this time, I might be a <i>little</i> bit worried. Just a little. Because my opinion is probably going to be extremely unpopular. <br/><br/><b>I honestly think Armentrout doe</b></span>
  <span id="freeText8891234139315731856" style="display:none">I am so sorry. I am SO sorry. <b>I am sooooo sorry.</b><br /><br />It's not often when I write a review and worry about having a difference of opinion from my friends - because if I had to worry, I'd have to do it for every single book review with the varied group of friends I have. Thankfully, I have awesome friends who don't mind me most of the time. However...this time, I might be a <i>little</i> bit worried. Just a little. Because my opinion is probably going to be extremely unpopular. <br /><br /><b>I honestly think Armentrout doesn't translate to adult writing with the same fluidity in which she writes YA.</b> This is the second adult book of hers (Serena's one year too old for my definition of NA) that I've read and had issues with. Her brand of sexual tension in YA is a great build which keeps the reader invested. Unfortunately, the way that the sexual detail transfers over to older characters reads so much like a copy of every single bad adult contemporary romance term which has already been over-used in thousands of other books. This is a case where I wish the author take a break from reading romance in order to completely forget the "Romance 101" generic terms so they can start over with their own personal descriptions.<br /><br />The sex scenes were not only cringe-worthy, but I failed to find them arousing on any level.<br /><br />Wombs were tightening. Bundles of nerves were tingling. Male parts were twitching. Sensations were felt down to the core. Even worse, words were used to describe Hunter's male part as a "thick and demanding proud length that jutted between us." Imaginary flavors were invented (can anyone taste like sunlight?). The obligatory "like a drug" reference was present (this time it was the taste of her skin). <br /><br /><b>But that's not what made me upset.</b> I was <i>appalled</i> by a scene in which (going to need to probably tag this as a spoiler) <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the guy was feeling up Serena while she was sleeping. He was touching all over her bared breasts while she was NOT awake, and he did NOT have her permission, other than her calling out IN HER SLEEP. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>This behavior is NOT okay.</b> I put part of the scene in the spoiler tag below. <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She was asleep and <b>definitely didn't know what she was asking for, but that soft plea was my undoing</b>.<br /><br />There wasn't a flicker of hesitation when it came to what I did next. I wasn't fooling myself or anyone. I wanted to touch her and so I did. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />What truly made me sad was that I started skimming by the second half because by the time I started learning more about the Luxen/Arum differences (which was the reason for me wanting to read the book in the first place, since I do like the Lux series and wanted to know more about the world), I was already checking out.<br /><br />I know that Lux book 4 is about to come out, but I might need to put a few weeks of distance between this book and the next, just so I can pick up the Lux book and enjoy it for what it is. <br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer431431312" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6695962768922207777"><b>
  <u>4-SWEET ALIEN BABIES EVERYWHERE-Stars</u>
</b><br/><br/>Move over Daemon, there's a new alien in town!!!<br/><i>Hello Hunter!</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380378342i/733926._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>In case you're wondering, yes, the Queen of Everything Jennifer L. Armentrout has done it again.<br/><br/>Hunter is definitely the baddest hot male character JLA has ever written.<i> EVER.</i><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393891ra/758421.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>"But damn, he was insanely hot for an... alien."</b><br/><br/>1. Hotness incarnated!!!<br/><br/>2. Has an ego the size of the planet .<br/><br/><b>"Not to burst your preconceived notions of me, but do I look like I care?"</b><br/><i>Yes, Hunter, we know. But I had to say</i></span>
  <span id="freeText6695962768922207777" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>4-SWEET ALIEN BABIES EVERYWHERE-Stars</u>
</b><br><br>Move over Daemon, there's a new alien in town!!!<br><i>Hello Hunter!</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380378342i/733926._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>In case you're wondering, yes, the Queen of Everything Jennifer L. Armentrout has done it again.<br><br>Hunter is definitely the baddest hot male character JLA has ever written.<i> EVER.</i><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393891ra/758421.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"But damn, he was insanely hot for an... alien."</b><br><br>1. Hotness incarnated!!!<br><br>2. Has an ego the size of the planet .<br><br><b>"Not to burst your preconceived notions of me, but do I look like I care?"</b><br><i>Yes, Hunter, we know. But I had to say my part, right?!</i><br><br>3. Arrogance that will put Daemon to shame.<br><br><b>"Look, things will be easier for you here if you get used to the way it needs to be."<br>This was going to be dandy. "And how is that?"<br>"You do as I say. It's that simple."</b><br><br>4. Dominant hottie. <i>Did I mentioned that before?!</i><br><br>5. Hunter was the badass of all badasses. I mean he was seriously like a super alien.<br>He kicked some major Luxen ass. And I'm not sure I should be so happy about that.<br>(Rooting for an Arum to kill Luxen was <i>WEIRD!!!</i>)<br><br>6. Hunter doesn't have "feelings". Especially not for humans or so he says.<br><br><b>"We may look human and even act it at times, but don't ever forget that we are not human."</b><br><br><i>And many, many more that I am just too wound up to think about.</i><br><br>It's really too bad he's 32.<br>That kinds of sucks since I'm only eighteen, I'm lucky Daemon isn't that old, otherwise.....pff...moving on....<br><br><i>
  <u>If Cam Hamilton from Waiting For You is such a cutie, Daemon Black from the Lux series is the heartthrob, then Hunter here from Obsession is the baddest and surely the hottest bad boy.</u>
</i><br><br>But those characteristics together with his sarcasm, cockiness, sexiness, funny side and ability to build up banter <i>made me melt onto the floor, burn into ashes and rise above the ground.<br>Repeatedly.</i><br>And just when he go over protective and alpha to Serena – Yay!<br>*girly giggles*.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393891ra/758422.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>-&gt;Team Arum vs Team Luxen<br>-&gt;Team Daemon vs Team Hunter<br>-&gt;Team Ca-- er wait wrong book.<br><br>So, you can sense my dilemna, right?!<br>*shakes fist at Jennifer*<br><br>He was a completely different person *ahem* alien than what we know the Arum to be.<br>Hunter was definitely the break out star of this book.<br>I loved his one liners!<br>He never failed to say something that sent me into lol mode.<br><br>Some of my favorite quotes from Hunter.........<br><br><b>“Mine. What in the fuckadeefuck had I meant by that? Mine? I stamped a claim on her after coming within seconds of killing her last night? Smooth.”<br><br>"Are you done acting like a psychotic, cracked-out Muppet baby?<br>Or do you need a couple more moments to return to sanity? I have all day. And you actually feel kind of good under me, so take your time."</b><br><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393891ra/758423.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I feel my review <s>will quickly</s> has become an epos about how I loved Hunter.<br>But, let's start it, shall we?<br>____________________________________________<br><br><u>
  <b>STORY:</b>
</u><br>So, when Hunter is asked to watch over a human, and protect Serena from the Luxen who are after her, he is clearly not happy with the task.<br>Hunter is all hard edges, and attitude.<br>She just happened to be in the wrong place, at the wrong time and saw something that has put her life in danger.<br>After her friend Mel was killed for the knowledge she possessed, Serena is on borrowed time. She knows that either the Luxen or the DOD are coming for her, she just isn't sure which, or when.<br>____________________________________________<br><br>The heroine, Serena, is funny, feisty, but took our dark hero to her heart in a wonderful way.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393891i/758424._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="550" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>No unnecessary hassle or sulking and no prolonged anxiety or indecision -<i> MAYBE too easily, I might say!!!</i><br><br><b>"Why can you listen then and not any other time?"<br>"Beacause I like to know what is going on, you giant dickhead."</b><br><br><br>And secondly, how in the name of mother loving hell can I get a hot alien for myself..........seriously, I freaking want one too......<br><br>And Thirdly, I thought we were supposed to hate the Arum?? I guess not...I mean, wow talk about a switcheroo, now I'm kinda hating the Luxen....<br><br>I was impressed with was how the Lux/Arum situation was handled. In the Lux series, the Arum are evul aliens intent on eating and killing the innocent Luxen…<br>But in this, the Luxen came across as the bad guys and the Arum just seemed like misunderstood underdogs.<br><br><i>It was actually kind of fun seeing things from the supposed bad guys perspective.</i><br><br><br><br>Lets not forget the steamy scenes that had me blushing and eyeing out my bookshelf *wink* and daydreaming my version of Hunter, a bookshelf .........*coughs*<br><br><b>“I can promise you that sex with me won’t be about long, soft pets or whispered words. I like it rough and raw, but your pleasure will always come first. Every single time.”</b><br><br>So, yes, let me tell you...Alien sex is mad hot. This book is more descriptive and mature than the ones in the Lux series.<br><br><b>“You are perfect for me, only me.”</b><br><i>Hunter</i> …....oh,yeah. JLA definitely delivers on the hotness in Obsession.<br><br><br>____________________________________________<br><br>And yes...oh yes...we got to see our favorite "good" badboy Luxen. It was minuscule, so tiny, but it was enough to make me grin like the Chesire cat in Alice in Wonderland.<br>Something about men in pain when it concerns their beloved makes me SO WARM.<br>It's sadistic but I clearly don't care.:P<br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>So, why, for-the-love-of-everything-sane <u>4 stars</u> you say?????</b><br><br>I liked Obsession I really did, but I didn't <i>lurve</i> it.<br>Maybe it's just because I was in a sort of reading funk or something but I did not love it as much as the other JLA books.<br><br>I am very partial to male book leads with a badboy streak. Ehem.<br>Daemon Black, for instance, thank you very much.<br>Sadly, Hunter, this man I had some issues with.<br>I liked him, yes, but he did not make my "book boyfriend list".<br><br>Then, there is Serena who I felt she was more "IN MAD CASE OF INSTA LUST" with Hunter, that too I might add only after a few days after the death of her best friend.<br>Shouldn't she be depressed???<br><br>And then, I felt like at the end of every fight, she put up a great front, but backed down in the end......<br>Now, where's the fun in that?<br>She should have been kicking his ass, BIG TIME!!!<br><i>Maybe its just the feminist in me talking!</i><br><br>However, after reading OBSESSION I keep asking myself who was Serena and who was Hunter?<br>OK, it is obvious that I do know who they are but I have a hollow feeling regarding their characters.<br><br>Even though the story was nice, I kind of didn’t get to know the characters as good as the characters in the Luxen novels.<br>WHAT EVER HAPPENED TO GETTING TO KNOW SOMEONE?<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393891ra/758425.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>You see, Serena and Hunter ? They were exactly like Katy and Daemon - but I seriously felt like Hunter was just moments away from calling Serena 'Kitten'.</i><br><br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>And now, the question of the year:</b>
</i> Daemon Black or Hunter…whose real name we actually do not know because it is unpronounceable?<br>This one is easy for me.<br>I will stick to Daemon!<br><br>They say there are two sides to every story and this book gives you a taste of that.<br>Take your preconceived notions and toss them out the window.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393891ra/758426.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This books makes you root for who you thought were the bad guys and makes you think there's a lot more to the story then you thought.<br>A MUST read for fans of Lux series.<br>I have a whole new outlook on both the Luxen and the Arum. I don't know who or what to believe?!?!<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Perhaps Hunter and Daemon should join forces to save Katy?!?!<br>What does all of this mean for Origin??<br>Will we see more of Hunter? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393891ra/758427.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Origin is like something we HAVE/NEED to understand any of this shit!<br><br><br><b>P.S:</b> Sorry if you feel like the review is written by two different people, but I promise its just me and <s>my insanity</s> inner self talking.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

Armentrout</a>'s <a href='http://jenniferarmentrout.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>blog:</a><br/><a href='http://jenniferarmentrout.blogspot.com/2012/10/obession.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <i>What can I tell you about Obsession?</i>
</a><br/>An Arum. Yes. You read that right.<br/>Obsession does take place in the same world that Katy and Daemon inhabit, <br/>Obsession is more mature, definitely targeted toward the older crowd. It's an adult romance, so you know what that means. <br/>Obsession will change what you think you know about the Luxens and Arums. <br/>There will be some crossover with certain characters from the Lux Series.<br/>Obsession takes place in-between Opal and the 4th </span>
  <span id="freeText13546220032055564287" style="display:none">On <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4476934.Jennifer_L__Armentrout" title="Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Jennifer L. Armentrout</a>'s <a href="http://jenniferarmentrout.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">blog:</a><br /><a href="http://jenniferarmentrout.blogspot.com/2012/10/obession.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <i>What can I tell you about Obsession?</i>
</a><br />An Arum. Yes. You read that right.<br />Obsession does take place in the same world that Katy and Daemon inhabit, <br />Obsession is more mature, definitely targeted toward the older crowd. It's an adult romance, so you know what that means. <br />Obsession will change what you think you know about the Luxens and Arums. <br />There will be some crossover with certain characters from the Lux Series.<br />Obsession takes place in-between Opal and the 4th Lux novel, which is called Origin.<br />Hunter and Serena are the lead characters in Obsession.<br /><br /><br /><u>
  <i>Update (05.12.2012):</i>
</u><br /><a href="http://jenniferarmentrout.blogspot.com/2012/05/teaser-alert.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #1</a><br /><a href="http://jenniferarmentrout.blogspot.com/2012/05/oh-yes-another-teaser.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #2</a><br /><i>-- (on <a href="http://jenniferarmentrout.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a>)</i><br /><br /><br /><u>
  <i>Update (12.12.2012):</i>
</u><br /><a href="http://deityisland.blogspot.com/2012/12/obsession-teaser.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #3:</a><br />“Not all of their kind came to Earth when our planets were destroyed. Tens of thousands are here, but there are hundreds of thousands out there. They will come eventually.” “And?” she asked, her arms loosening and falling to her sides. “And humans will be glad that there are Arums on this planet when that day comes.”<br /><i>-- (on <a href="http://deityisland.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Deity Island</a>)</i><br /><br /><br /><u>
  <i>Update (24.12.2012):</i>
</u><br /><a href="https://twitter.com/JLArmentrout/status/282277036670730240" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #4:</a><br />"We’re in their world, babe. Don’t ya worry about the Luxen boy in there with Luc. Worry about yourself.”<br /><a href="https://twitter.com/JLArmentrout/status/282244202715291648" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #5:</a><br />"Luxens were like galactic Pringles in a f**ked up way. Once you popped one, you just couldn’t stop."<br /><i>-- (on <a href="https://twitter.com/JLArmentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">twitter</a>)</i><br /><br /><br /><u>
  <i>Update (03.02.2013):</i>
</u><br /><a href="http://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/posts/327919427309626" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #5:</a><br />There wasn’t any kind of trouble that I couldn’t ass kick my way out of, so whatever.<br /><i>-- (on <a href="http://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout?fref=ts" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>)</i><br /><br /><a href="http://www.jenniferarmentrout.com/obsessiontease/" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #6:</a><br />***<br />“You don’t look very apologetic.”<br />I frowned. “Well, I am. Things are kind of… messed up. And you knocked me out. And you’re half naked—”<br />“Have you looked in the mirror?” he cut in. “You’re just as naked as I am. And I didn’t throw anything at your head.”<br />Glancing down at myself, I cringed. Somehow I’d forgotten that I was in my shirt and undies. Flushing all over again, I wanted to dart behind something, but I folded my arms. “I didn’t throw anything at your head. I was—”<br />“Do you always overreact like this?”<br />Oh my God, if he interrupted me one more time I was going to throw something at his head. “I woke up in a strange place, kidnapped by an alien. I can’t even believe I’m explaining why I overreacted. What were you doing in my room anyway?”<br />He mimicked my stance. “Correction: this is my house and therefore this is my room. Not that I need to explain myself, I was checking to make sure everything was secure outside.”<br />“But you did kidnap me.”<br />“I did not.”<br />I threw up my hands. “What’s all this? Where am I?”<br />“West Virginia.”<br />My mouth dropped open. Oh, my God, this couldn’t be happening. “I’m in a different time zone? Are you fuc—”<br />Hunter threw up his hand, silencing me. The tip of my tongue literally burned to lay into him. “What the hell is that noise?”<br />Before I could respond, he stalked past the bed and entered the bathroom.<br />“Jesus! What are you trying to do in here?” His voice carried from the bathroom. “Giving the floor a bath?” he demanded.<br />I searched desperately for my jeans, but came up empty.<br />Hunter returned, hands on his hips. Too late. “Seriously?”<br />“I forgot I turned the faucet on. Geez, you’re grumpy.”<br />“And you’re already turning out to be a huge pain in my thigh.”<br />“Look, I’m really sorry about that. Okay? I’ve been through some really traumatic events here recently and yes, I might have overreacted.” I struggled with my patience. “And I really would just like to know where my pants are.”<br />“Your pants were folded on the corner of the bed. You probably knocked them on the floor.”<br />What? I wanted to check, but I so wasn’t bending down in my panties in front of him. “And how did they get off me and folded on the bed?”<br />“I did it. Thought you’d be more comfortable.”<br />Oh geez, I had no idea what to think about that. A thank you so wasn’t in order though. He did undress me while I was unconsciousness for crying out loud. My entire body felt red-hot. “I’m not going to say thank you for that.”<br />“Not like I’d expect that common courtesy from you,” he replied, his pale eyes dancing… with what? Anger? Amusement? “After all you never thanked me for saving your ass—a pretty ass at that. So I can add inconsiderate to your glowing list of attributes. Put that right next to: overreacts, acts first and then thinks, drama—”<br />“Oh, go fuc–”<br />“You do not want to finish that sentence,” Hunter warned. His voice low enough to send warning shivers down my spine.<br />****<br /><i>-- (on <a href="http://jenniferarmentrout.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a>)</i><br /><br /><br /><u>
  <i>Update (04/01/'13):</i>
</u><br /><a href="http://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/posts/349128361855399" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #7:</a><br />“Are you done acting like a psychotic, cracked-out muppet baby?” he demanded. <br /><i>-- (on <a href="http://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout?fref=ts" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>)</i><br /><br /><br /><u>
  <i>Update (05/09/'13):</i>
</u><br /><a href="https://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/posts/360964930671742" rel="nofollow noopener">Q&amp;A about Obsession:</a><br />1. The main characters are Hunter and Selena. <br />2. This book is not a Lux novel, but it does take place in the same "world" as the Lux series. It is a companion novel. <br />3. Characters from the Lux series will crossover into this novel. <br />4. The events in this book take place between Opal and Origin to give you an idea of timeline<br />5. This is an ADULT novel, meaning if you are a youngin, this book is not for you. Because of that, Obsession can be read w/ or w/out reading the Lux series. <br />6. Hunter is probably my second favorite guy I've ever written<br />7. This is a digital release only.<br /><br /><br /><u>
  <i>Update (05/11/'13):</i>
</u><br /><a href="https://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/posts/362166157218286" rel="nofollow noopener">Some lines from Obsession:</a><br />Patience was a virtue I found pointless. ~Hunter<br /><br />My kind *did* like to covet pretty, little things. ~Hunter <br /><br />“Are you done acting like a psychotic, cracked-out Muppet baby? I have all day. And u actually feel kind of good under me, so take your time.” ~ Hunter<br /><br />Oh hell, the first taste, the first drop of her essence was a deep, firm stroke to the fire that burned inside me. ~Hunter</span>

<div id="review_2421873134" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2421873134" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2421873134?book_show_action=true">Jun 12, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=space-aliens">space-aliens</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=3sciencefiction-lovestories">3sciencefiction-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=demons">demons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2421873134" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7346885982530275150"><b>
  <i>“This is not your problem.”<br/>“You are my problem.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>I loved the first part of the book when Serena meets Hunter and we learn many things about Arum together with her. It was interesting to realise that you need always to look at situations from a different prospective and judge only after you see what every different character thinks .<br/><br/><b>
  <i>The good guys really weren't typical. They really weren't the good guys at all, but if I discovered anything, there was no such thing as white and black. There</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText7346885982530275150" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“This is not your problem.”<br />“You are my problem.” </i>
</b><br /><br />I loved the first part of the book when Serena meets Hunter and we learn many things about Arum together with her. It was interesting to realise that you need always to look at situations from a different prospective and judge only after you see what every different character thinks .<br /><br /><b>
  <i>The good guys really weren't typical. They really weren't the good guys at all, but if I discovered anything, there was no such thing as white and black. There was a lot of gray in the middle. </i>
</b><br /><br />The second part after these two visit Luc, I think it has a slower pace and it did not grab my attention that much. And Luc steals their thunder.<br /><br /><b>
  <i> “Oh, shimmer down, Hunter. You're too testy. How many times have I've told you that you need to chill out, take a vacay. Disney World is really fun this time of the year. you should check it out.” </i>
</b><br /><br />Arum are not always bad, although they are darkness.<br />Luxen are not always good, although they are light.<br /><br />The most important reality is that one can counterattack the other. <br /><br /><b>
  <i> “That´s an alien. I´m an alien. We´re aliens. Aliens everywhere, acutally, which is why we have to leave. I´m sure someone called the police by now.” </i>
</b><br /><br />Actually, I am not sure whether you should read this book before Origin and Opposition because it definitely contains lots of spoilers . I read it after I finished the Lux series and I think it is the best way to enjoy the book.<br /><br />The above comments are in terms of the general story.<br /><br />Now, about Hunter and Selena.....<br />I loved the possessiveness and protectiveness of Hunter. He tries so hard to protect her from everyone who wants to hurt her. He does not hesitate to fight Luxen, Humans - even other Arum. Of course it will take him some time to realise that he loves her and that although he is alien, he can still react as a human and have human feelings.<br /><br /><b>
  <i> “Shit. Next I’ll hold her hand and start talking about butterflies and rainbows. Fuck me.” </i>
</b><br /><br />On the other hand Selena behaves as a “too stupid to live” heroine many times, but you don't really dislike her. She is certainly cute in her attempts to show some backbone against the more dangerous and stronger predators.<br /><br /><b>
  <i> “Are you done acting like a psychotic, cracked-out Muppet baby?" he asked, and I could tell by the way his fingers spasmed around my wrists, he really wanted to shake me. <br />"Or do you need a couple more moments to return to sanity? I have all day. And you actually feel kind of good under me, so take your time.” </i>
</b><br /><br />Together, Hunter and Selena are hot and steamy. It may remind you Daemon and Katy's initial dynamics.<br /><br /><b>
  <i> “We stared at each other for several moments, neither of us speaking or moving, and then I was in front of her, pulling her to my chest, breathing in her scent as I went down on my knees, bring her with me. Her arms went around me and she held on just as tightly as I held her. It was then when I realized I was still in my true form. She was light against my darkness.<br /><br />Serena hadn't backed away or hesitated. She accepted me, all of me. She always had.” </i>
</b><br /><br />This is a New Adult book (not like the main Lux series that is Young Adult), so expect sex between these two early in the book and in details. And frequently.<br />Sometimes I think that this book tries too hard to have a New Adult feel and be a book for grown ups – not successfully always.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7346885982530275150" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/598777152?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=para-dystopian-sci-fi-fantasy">para-dystopian-sci-fi-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer598777152" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7659773699418855311"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418882i/829818._SY540_.jpg' width='320' height='399' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Good vs. Evil<br/><br/>Light vs. Darkness<br/><br/>Luxen vs. Arum</b><br/><br/>Well, I thought I had it all figured out…Boy was I wrong!<br/><br/>Jennifer L. Armentrout is a genius! She took what fans of the Lux Series know to be the truth from the view point of Daemon Black and his siblings and blew it to smithereens! <br/> <br/>When you said the word Arum to me before reading this book, I would immediately associate it with images and words like evil, darkness, self-serving and of course <b>THE ENEMY</b>. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>”We’ve always been seen as a weapon. That’s w</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText7659773699418855311" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418882i/829818._SY540_.jpg" width="320" height="399" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Good vs. Evil<br><br>Light vs. Darkness<br><br>Luxen vs. Arum</b><br><br>Well, I thought I had it all figured out…Boy was I wrong!<br><br>Jennifer L. Armentrout is a genius! She took what fans of the Lux Series know to be the truth from the view point of Daemon Black and his siblings and blew it to smithereens! <br> <br>When you said the word Arum to me before reading this book, I would immediately associate it with images and words like evil, darkness, self-serving and of course <b>THE ENEMY</b>. <br><br><b>
  <i>”We’ve always been seen as a weapon. That’s what we are.”</i>
</b><br><br>After reading <i>Obsession</i>, the first thoughts that now enters my mind when the word Arum is mentioned is kick ass, sexy as hell, sarcastic and fantastic and his name is…Hunter.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418882i/829819._SX540_.jpg" width="340" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story was a definite 5 stars for me from the story line to the terrific dialogue to the <b>HOOOOOTTTTT</b> sex scenes. <br><br><b>
  <i>”I can promise you that sex with me won’t be about long, soft pets, or whispered words. I like it rough and raw, but your pleasure will always come first. Every single time.”</i>
</b><br><br>The story is about Serena Cross who’s best friend, Melanie overhears and witnesses some crazy things that are really important (we're talking world domination here) to a lot of top secret groups.<br> <br><b>
  <i>”WHY ARE YOU HELPING ME?”<br><br>Helping her wasn’t a huge risk. It was the nail in the universal coffin”</i>
</b><br><br>Serena finds that her life is in danger by….oh I can’t even say it's still crazy to me. Anyhow, she finds herself under the protection of an Arum named Hunter in his Virginian home. These two had tons of hysterical banter and loads of chemistry. <br> <br><b>
  <i>“Never in my life had I been more frustrated. Go figure it wouldn't be with a human but a freaking alien. At least I now knew that the male species were asses no matter what planet they hailed from.” </i>
</b><br><br>I’m not giving anything away but I’ll say that the only opponent Hunter lost to in this book was little old cupid!<br><br>The story is told in alternating povs and doesn’t end with a cliffhanger. I completely inhaled this book and I still want more…Hint Hint. <br><br><b>Side Notes:</b><br>Daemon needs to get Hunter’s cell number because this sexy Arum could have Katy rescued in seconds!<br><br>Luc what the hell is he? The missing link or is there another species involved here?<br><br>This series is a <b>MUST</b> for fans of the Lux Series. <br><br>Did you really have any doubts? <br><br>Come on, it’s Jennifer L. Armentrout!</span>

<div id="review_630009243" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/630009243" />
    <a title="Ferdy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy"><img alt="Ferdy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487898103p2/4596358.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/630009243?book_show_action=true">Jun 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ferdy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ferdy" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy">Ferdy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781622661602" href="/book/show/17910374-obsession">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=abusive-hero">abusive-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=blah">blah</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=aliens">aliens</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=awful-love-interest">awful-love-interest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=rubbish">rubbish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=blah-romance">blah-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=tstl-heroine">tstl-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=hero-dick-to-heroine">hero-dick-to-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=boring">boring</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=boring-crap-hero">boring-crap-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer630009243" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2480880464514666376"><b>Some Spoilers</b><br/><br/>Predictable, cheesy and rather offensive. The story, the characters and the romance were pretty much exactly the same as all other PNR books except with aliens. I have to admit that I did find it somewhat entertaining up until the 'hero' got all rapey. <br/><br/>-The main reason it got one star instead of zero was because the heroine wasn't a virgin. I had been worried that JLA (like most female YA/UF/PNR authors) had some sort of weird thing for young virgin heroines and manslut heroes… But </span>
  <span id="freeText2480880464514666376" style="display:none"><b>Some Spoilers</b><br /><br />Predictable, cheesy and rather offensive. The story, the characters and the romance were pretty much exactly the same as all other PNR books except with aliens. I have to admit that I did find it somewhat entertaining up until the 'hero' got all rapey. <br /><br />-The main reason it got one star instead of zero was because the heroine wasn't a virgin. I had been worried that JLA (like most female YA/UF/PNR authors) had some sort of weird thing for young virgin heroines and manslut heroes… But thankfully that wasn't the case in <i>Obsession</i>. I think JLA leaves most of her sexual double standards and sexism for her YA books. <br /><br />-I wasn't a fan of the heroine, Serena. She wasn't a totally bad character, it was just that she was the same old bland-typical-boring-modest-do-goody-heroine. Basically the standard placeholder heroine.<br /><br />-It was dumb and laughable that a mere few days after Serena's best friend (and the only person she had left in the world) died, she was getting all hot and bothered over some random guy. Instead of grieving for her friend, all she did was think about how hot the hero (Hunter) was, and how lusty he made her. <br /><br />-I was so sick of Serena blushing every time Hunter so much as looked at her. She was a grown woman for fuck's sake yet she still blushed like a tween girl over <i>every</i> lame innuendo or cheesy look.<br /><br />-WTF was with Serena having sex the same day she was almost raped by that random evul guy?!<br /><br />-Hunter was a douchey-rapey-sterotypical-forgettable-fucker of a hero. It was sickening how he thought it was okay to feel up girls in their sleep. Ugh.<br /><br />-I really hated that Hunter groped Serena when she was sleeping. She was ASLEEP, she wasn't able to give fucking permission but rapey Hunter still felt her up anyway… That's sexual assault. What's with all these authors writing rape as if it's something sexy and hot. Ugh.<br /><br />-A note to romance authors… A hero being arrogant, rapey and bossy doesn't equal a bad boy personality or a personality for that matter.<br /><br />-The romance between Hunter and Serena was shallow and dull. Serena kept banging on about Hunter's looks, and Hunter kept banging on about how feisty Serena was and how she had great hair. They had no deeper connection or further development than that.<br /><br />-One thing I was impressed with was how the Lux/Arum situation was handled. In the Lux series, the Arum are evul aliens intent on eating and killing the innocent Luxen… But in this, the Luxen or Lux or whatever came across as the bad guys and the Arum just seemed like misunderstood underdogs. It was actually kind of fun seeing things from the supposed bad guys perspective.<br /><br />-I didn't like that the heroine's name was Serena, it just reminded me of Serena from <i>Gossip Girl</i>.<br /><br />-The male characters insulting each other and themselves by using the word vagina pissed me off… WTF?! Because vaginas are so lame. FUCK OFF with all the sexism and female hating!!<br /><br />-Am I meant to find guys that wear leather pants sexy or something? I don't. <br /><br />All in all, rubbish. It might have been okay if Hunter wasn't a rapey fuck, and if the characters had some depth.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2480880464514666376" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1695806375" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1695806375" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer347466702429374690">Ok, this book officially proved that the Arum can be just as gorgeous, awesome, and selfless as the Luxen. I'm still in a state of shock after this book, wow. <br/>Even though I thought this book was really short, it still went into details about the Luxen and Arum that I didn't even read about in the Lux series, which I found super cool! <br/><br/>After this book Daemon and Dawson are not the only two aliens I have major crushes on, now Hunter is definitely added to that list<3 <br/><br/>Awesome stand-alone Arum story,</span>
  <span id="freeText347466702429374690" style="display:none">Ok, this book officially proved that the Arum can be just as gorgeous, awesome, and selfless as the Luxen. I'm still in a state of shock after this book, wow. <br />Even though I thought this book was really short, it still went into details about the Luxen and Arum that I didn't even read about in the Lux series, which I found super cool! <br /><br />After this book Daemon and Dawson are not the only two aliens I have major crushes on, now Hunter is definitely added to that list&lt;3 <br /><br />Awesome stand-alone Arum story, highly recommend to anyone, especially fans of the lux series(:</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/434652230?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristalia " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristalia " href="/user/show/5705623-kristalia">Kristalia </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=me-likey-mucho">me-likey-mucho</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=they-are-so-awesome-hot-and-stuff">they-are-so-awesome-hot-and-stuff</a>,
