        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer434652230" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7332217047021340747"><br/><b>Final rating: 4/5 stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “That´s an alien. I´m an alien. We´re aliens. Aliens everywhere, acutally, which is why we have to leave. I´m sure someone called the police by now.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394381i/759329._SX540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>If i remember correctly, <b>
  <i>my brain and heart and body belonged to Luxen race... But not anymore! </i>
</b>I am officially <b>
  <i>switching sides!</i>
</b><br/><br/>Overall, <b>
  <i> I freaking loved it </i>
</b> :D Despite it's faults, i still loved it. I had so much <b>
  <i> fun reading</i>
</b> it and i was so <b>
  <i> captivated by it </i>
</b> that i couldn't wait to see ho</span>
  <span id="freeText7332217047021340747" style="display:none"><br><b>Final rating: 4/5 stars</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “That´s an alien. I´m an alien. We´re aliens. Aliens everywhere, acutally, which is why we have to leave. I´m sure someone called the police by now.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394381i/759329._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>If i remember correctly, <b>
  <i>my brain and heart and body belonged to Luxen race... But not anymore! </i>
</b>I am officially <b>
  <i>switching sides!</i>
</b><br><br>Overall, <b>
  <i> I freaking loved it </i>
</b> :D Despite it's faults, i still loved it. I had so much <b>
  <i> fun reading</i>
</b> it and i was so <b>
  <i> captivated by it </i>
</b> that i couldn't wait to see how the story ends!<br><br><b>*spoiler free review*</b><br><br>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●<br><br>First things first: i suggest you do <b>
  <i>read Lux series before reading this one.</i>
</b> <br><br>It's timeline is set<b>
  <i> between <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13362536.Opal__Lux___3_" title="Opal (Lux, #3) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Opal</a> &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13644052.Origin__Lux___4_" title="Origin (Lux, #4) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Origin</a>, </i>
</b> and it will <b>
  <i> spoil you </i>
</b> - there is no chance that you will miss who appeared from the Lux series and you will just pointlessly spoil yourself. <br><br>And also, <b>
  <i> read it between them just so you understand both sides,</i>
</b> both Lux and Arum, and story of Obsession is closely connected to it.<br><br>But, <b>
  <i> if you have never read any of the Lux books, you can read it and it will still be fun! :D</i>
</b> <br><br>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●<br><br><b>
  <u>So how come i switched sides and now root for Arum?</u>
</b><br><br>I know, i know, Arum race is <b>
  <i>eviiiiiiiil</i>
</b>. Or so we have <b>
  <i> been led to believe by Luxen race</i>
</b> ... And this book proves it. You will now think which race is good and which is evil. Answer is:<b>
  <i> both races are good, and both are equally evil</i>
</b>. <br><br><br>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●<br><br><u>
  <b> Why 4 stars then?</b>
</u><br><br>Because the characters <b>
  <i> reminded me too much of Daemon and Katy</i>
</b> from Lux... (more about it in <b>
  <i> characters </i>
</b> section). But i also think characters lacked more depth then they were given. <br><br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>STORY</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br><i>In a universe, far away, there were two planets, with two different races. Lux race, a race of Light, and Arum race, a race of shadows. And they are in never ending war. Destroying the planets in process, they settle on Earth...</i><br><br>When Mel, Serena's best friend, finds out that her boyfriend is an alien, she tries to convince Serena to believe her. Serena is sure that Mel is wrong because she can't believe in it...until Mel gets killed right in front of Serena's eyes. By a Luxen. <br><br>Hunter is one of the Arum, the alien race which lives to kill Lux race. Hunter is the agent of Department of Defense, for the sole purpose of killing and getting rid of Luxen race who go stray. So when he is told that he needs to be a bodyguard to a human... things get really crazy.<br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>CHARACTERS</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Serena</u>
  </i>
</b>:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394381i/759331._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Serena is a human, who due to unfortunate events, ends up being with alien. Her best friend is murdered and government wants her safe... for now. To do so, they assigned Hunter to protect her.<br><br>Serena was interesting, but to tell you the truth, i didn't really like her much. I don't hate her either, but i have to say i loved when she argued and pissed off Hunter, because it was too much fun!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You shouldn’t be attracted to me.”<br>“What?” I threw up my hands. “You cannot be serious.”<br>Hunter arched a brow. “Do I not look serious to you?”<br>“You look like an arrogant, pompous ass!” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>or even better: <br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>”Your arrogance is rooted in stupidity.”<br>“And your lifespan is getting shorter by the second.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Anyway, she was not a bad character at all, though i have to say that one thing bothered me about her. Her best friend died, and all she does is lust over a man... I expected she is going to be extremely depressed or something, because it would be normal reaction... Death of someone close is not something you can just ignore, even if it was a man in question. (it kind of got on my nerves the fact that she always blushed around him...seriously?)<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “Never in my life had I been more frustrated. Go figure it wouldn't be with a human but a freaking alien. At least I now knew that the male species were asses no matter what planet they hailed from.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>She reminds me too much of Katy from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12578077.Obsidian__Lux___1_" title="Obsidian (Lux, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Lux</a> series, and that is what bothered me the most. She is basically the older version of her.<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Hunter</u>
  </i>
</b>:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394381i/759332._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Hunter is a ruthless assassin, and he is one of the strongest of his kind. He is there to eliminate any threats and he is happy to do that... And then, he gets the duty of "baby sitting" one of the humans, and he doesn't know whether it should amuse him, or bother him. Which leads to akward situations where he <i> accidentally</i> feeds on her. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> I knocked her out . Again . Aw fuck. </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Not in the vampire kind of way, but his race feeds on energy of both Humans and Luxen. <br><br>My ladies (and gentlemen), Hunter is the <b>ultimate anti hero ever written </b>. He is extremely arrogant, self confident and cocky, straight forward and completely frustrating at times! ... But he is also cold, controlling... and he always gets what he wants. Not to mention, he is definitely not a romantic type <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ (being all rapey and stuff) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> Damn, Serena was a really, really good-looking woman, but when she smiled? Hell, she was hands down beautiful.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>But Hunter is also protective of Serena, which is the only good thing i loved about him. Except for being hot alien, who knows how to cook and who can craft stuff. And, as the time passes, he changes for better... Because of Serena.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Life’s rarely fair, sweetheart.” He slid his hands over my thighs as his lips brushed the curve of my jaw once more. “We’ve always been seen as a weapon. That’s what we are.”<br>“No.” Heat unfurled inside me, spreading sizzling shivers. “You’re more than a weapon, Hunter. So much more.”<br>“With you?” His voice was thick. “I am more, but not with anyone else.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And if you thought Daemon Black was horrible, on scale from 1 to 10, Daemon would be 5, and Hunter would get 10. Hunter is a meaner, scarier and definitely older version of Daemon. It's hard for me to like him or hate him, because i do hate and like him in the same time, if it makes any sense.<br><br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>OVERALL</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>It was... well, interesting and i enjoyed it really much. I just wish it was a series like Lux, because i wouldn't reading adult series about Arum :D<br><br>And if you are fan of Lux, definitely check it out. And if you want interesting romance with really bad boy type, this is for you.<br><br><br>Over and out. </b><br><br>____________________________________________<br><br>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●<br>____________________________________________ <br><br><b>REVIEW(S) RELATED TO THIS BOOK:</b><br><br>◈ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/283274430" rel="nofollow noopener"> Opal (Lux, #3) <br> </a> <br><br><br>❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤ ❤<br><br>Buddy read with Georgia, Kristina and Sandra ♥<br>thanx for inviting me, we had fun drolling over Hunter ♥♥♥<br><br>✦<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/426819520" rel="nofollow noopener">Georgia's review</a><br>✦<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/478950930" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristina's review</a><br>✦<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/531215323" rel="nofollow noopener">Sandra's review</a><br><br><br><b>
  <i>This review can be found on my blog: <a href="http://infinity-of-time.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">infinity-of-time.blogspot.com</a> also known as... </i>
</b><br><a href="http://infinity-of-time.blogspot.com/2013/06/obsession-by-jennifer-l-armentrout.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380363317i/714576.png" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_629982196" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/629982196" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/629982196?book_show_action=true">Jun 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=is-getting-hot-in-here">is-getting-hot-in-here</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=paranornal-stuff">paranornal-stuff</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer629982196" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18156864141752446468">Initially I didn’t want to read this book because, let’s be real: The main male is an Arum. After being completely in love with the Lux Series, it felt like I was betraying Daemon Black. <br/>Well, now I’m glad I got over it, as this is a really good book. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380367810ra/720307.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So, this book takes place in the world of the Lux Series, where aliens are very real… and very sexy. <br/>Serena sees her best friend getting killed, because she saw too much: she saw Luxens in their true form and talking about something that no one sho</span>
  <span id="freeText18156864141752446468" style="display:none">Initially I didn’t want to read this book because, let’s be real: The main male is an Arum. After being completely in love with the Lux Series, it felt like I was betraying Daemon Black. <br>Well, now I’m glad I got over it, as this is a really good book. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380367810ra/720307.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, this book takes place in the world of the Lux Series, where aliens are very real… and very sexy. <br>Serena sees her best friend getting killed, because she saw too much: she saw Luxens in their true form and talking about something that no one should know. Serena didn’t believed in her at first instance, because, let’s face it: aliens that light up like bulbs? <i>Really??</i><br>But the Luxens didn’t really care about what she believed or not and she could be a risk, so, they send someone to kill her.<br><br>For reasons that I don’t want to explain now, the DOD hired Hunter, an Arum at their service, to protect her. Displeased is a very soft word for what he felt about having to <i>babysitting her when he could be doing so many better things.</i><br>But well, she’s not very pleased either and she wants to make sure he knows that. <br>The time passes, she’s in danger, their alone and attracted to each other, and things start to happen. If you want to know more you really have to go read the book, now. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423709ra/844339.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What can I say? Serena is a pretty good heroine, Hunter is sexy as sin and for some blissful moments we get to see our favorite little luxen, Daemon, who else? <br>The book has a great story and raises a lot of questions to the people who follow the Lux Series: Who are the bad guys after all? Luxens or Arums? <br>And are we, human people, really that naïve? <br><br>Well, another extremely good reading. But then again, I don’t think I’ll ever be disappointed with a book of this author. <br>You may go read it, for real now. ;) <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="18156864141752446468" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1782489126036425889"><b>LOVED IT!!!!!!!!! 5 EXTRATERRESTRIAL STARS!!!!!!</b><br/><br/>Another alien masterpiece by Jennifer Armentrout!!!! Now before you start this book, it would be very helpful if you read her <b>Luxen</b> series first. This book is a take off on that series, showing us readers the other side of the coin, from the eyes of the enemy. And what a delicious glimpse it is into the mind and the life of the <b>Arum</b>. <br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/slender_man_into_darkness_by_bear_shaped_ham-d3crv4l.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909596i/3181583._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo slender_man_into_darkness_by_bear_shaped_ham-d3crv4l.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>The book starts out with a bang and a murder. Serena Cross’ best friend Mel, a wild and crazy fun-l</span>
  <span id="freeText1782489126036425889" style="display:none"><b>LOVED IT!!!!!!!!! 5 EXTRATERRESTRIAL STARS!!!!!!</b><br><br>Another alien masterpiece by Jennifer Armentrout!!!! Now before you start this book, it would be very helpful if you read her <b>Luxen</b> series first. This book is a take off on that series, showing us readers the other side of the coin, from the eyes of the enemy. And what a delicious glimpse it is into the mind and the life of the <b>Arum</b>. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/slender_man_into_darkness_by_bear_shaped_ham-d3crv4l.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909596i/3181583._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo slender_man_into_darkness_by_bear_shaped_ham-d3crv4l.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The book starts out with a bang and a murder. Serena Cross’ best friend Mel, a wild and crazy fun-loving girl has a wild night out and finds herself hooked up with the Senator’s son. She wakes up shortly after, overhearing a conversation between him and his brother. She is intrigued by their strange conversation, and is then quickly shocked by the altercation she witnesses between the two. She hears and sees some things that will soon seal her fate and lead to her untimely death. <br><br>However, before this all plays out, she manages to share her unfortunate sighting with her best friend Serena. Of course, Serena doesn’t believe her, who would? What she saw was impossible, right? Well apparently not… and soon Serena finds herself in danger as well, and on the run, with no one to trust.<br><br><b>Hunter</b> is an Arum who has sort of “sold out” to the man, and started working for the DOD (Department of Defense). He has been assigned to watch over Serena, and to find out just how much she knows. He is not happy about this assignment, but is accepts it reluctantly. However once he seeks her out, he will soon find he must fight his own instincts to keep her safe. <br><br>He is an Arum after all, a killer. And his cravings are testing the limits of his self-control. He is instantly struck with her appearance and vulnerability, and finds himself drawn to her. But his cravings go beyond sex. He has a hunger to feed from her as well, and if he indulges this need, he will kill her himself. This he cannot allow to happen. But his frustration proves to be intense, way beyond what he was prepared to deal with. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/AbSTRACT_T.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909596i/3181584.jpg" alt=" photo AbSTRACT_T.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>He also finds himself feeling protective of her…possessive. A feeling totally new to him. She is a human after all. He is Arum, and he doesn’t need this shit. Arum are only about self-preservation and pleasure. But fuck him, he was falling for her…<br><br><b>
  <i>And if I was honest, I was fucking terrified of the idea. Somehow, in the relatively short time I’d known Serena, she had wiggled her way into my cold body. She was my light, my warmth, and I wasn’t ready to let her go.</i>
</b><br><br><b>Serena</b> Cross at the age of 23 had already lived through some pretty rough times. Her mother had been murdered during a botched robbery attempt when she was a freshman in college, and her father was never a part of her life. She found herself young and alone at a very young age. For this reason, she had relied heavily on the love and support of her best friend Mel. So when Mel is also taken from her life, she is forced to stand alone and fight for her life. <br><br>So when Hunter shows up to offer up protection, Serena is not very accepting of his help, in fact she is completely freaked out by him. He has a formidable presence and then there is the fact that he is NOT HUMAN! Yes, he appears and acts human…and a freaking hot one at that, and he did save her life, but his cold demeanor and prickly personality have her questioning his loyalty. Not to mention his intense need to feed from her.<br><br><b>
  <i>At least I knew that the male species were asses no matter what planet they hailed from.</i>
</b><br><br>The chemistry between these two is white hot and the fast building sexual tension is completely addictive, as is the verbal banter between them. I absolutely LOVE this couple!!!! I was literally glued to the book!!!! I never wanted to put it down…damn real life, always getting in the way!!!! Hunter is soooooo fucking HOT, and sweet with Serena. But he has just that right amount of domination and forcefulness in his seduction…just fucking PERFECTION!!!!!! I’m totally in LOVE with this guy!!!!!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>”You’re so cocky.”<br>“Ah, don’t say anything with the word cock in it.”<br>“What?” She giggled. “Will I wake the slumbering beast?”<br>“The slumbering beast is always awake around you.” And hell if the “beast” wasn’t stirring.</i>
</b><br><br>And Serena was tough, not your typical weepy pitiful heroine. She was tougher than nails….and would stand up for herself and her beliefs, even when I thought she was making a stupid decision. And yes, she was stupid…more than once, but she owned it, and she didn’t wine about it. She knew she made some bad choices and she admitted it… I respected her for that. Overall, I liked her…a lot!!!! And she overcame some serious shit in this book, and stood tall and claimed her man!!! (I mean her alien!!!) <br><br><b>
  <i>It wasn’t that I was necessarily stronger that them. Luxen were formidable opponents. I was fighting differently that I ever had before. It wasn’t about the age-old battle of Arum versus Luxen. I wasn’t fighting to feed or to work off aggression. I wasn’t fighting because I was told or was obligated.<br>I was fighting for Serena.<br>She meant everything to me.<br>Knowing that, fully understanding what that meant, I was on a motherfucking warpath.</i>
</b><br><br>I can’t say enough about this book, or Jennifer Armentrout!!!! I love this whole series, and I’m really intrigued with where the story is headed, with the Project Eagle and all that is involves!!!!! And yes… this book definitely had me feeling guilty for pulling for the Arum against the Luxen!!!!! I totally betrayed Daemon… and I couldn’t help it. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Hunter’s fierce reclaiming of his woman at the end was just magnificent to witness!!!!! Take THAT Senator Vanderson, you asswipe!!!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>
  <i>Her scream echoed through my soul, and at that moment, I knew I had one. Human or not, it rocked me to my very core.</i>
</b><br><br>I LOVE LOVE LOVED this book, and highly recommend it…. But remember, read the Luxen series first!!!!! Great book!!!!!!!!!!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>Serena hadn’t backed away or hesitated. She accepted me, all of me. She always had.<br>I slipped into my human form, cradling her against me. The words, they came out easier than I ever thought they would. “I love you.”</i>
</b><br><br><br>here are my pics...<br><br><b>Hunter<br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/A-0DmycCIAAPBUtjpg-large.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909596i/3181585.jpg" alt=" photo A-0DmycCIAAPBUtjpg-large.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Serena Cross</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/tumblr_m8b5e0UfBf1rvjdseo1_500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909596i/3181586.jpg" alt="Erin Heatherton photo tumblr_m8b5e0UfBf1rvjdseo1_500.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer631752152" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17948128087246591918">★★★★★5 Hunter-Gave-Me-A-Serious-Lady-Boner Stars★★★★★<br/><br/>Before I started reading Obsession, I didn't think there was any way I was going to end up liking an Arum. The Lux books teach us that the Arums are basically the exact opposite of the Luxen. Arums are dark, evil, and devoid of emotion where the Luxen are light, good, and more than capable of caring for each other and the human population. This book takes all of your preconceived notions and throws them out the window!<br/><br/>Serena Cross's life explo</span>
  <span id="freeText17948128087246591918" style="display:none">★★★★★5 Hunter-Gave-Me-A-Serious-Lady-Boner Stars★★★★★<br><br>Before I started reading Obsession, I didn't think there was any way I was going to end up liking an Arum. The Lux books teach us that the Arums are basically the exact opposite of the Luxen. Arums are dark, evil, and devoid of emotion where the Luxen are light, good, and more than capable of caring for each other and the human population. This book takes all of your preconceived notions and throws them out the window!<br><br>Serena Cross's life explodes when she witnesses her best friend being murdered by an alien. Her best friend learned some very incriminating information about a senator and his family and passed some of this information along to Serena before she was killed. The Department of Defense is trying to determine what Serena knows but they will have to make sure that she is protected from the aliens who killed her friend in order to get that information and decide what to do with her. Hunter is an Arum that is given the task of protecting Serena. He normally could care less about the DOD and any humans, but Serena is different. He seems drawn to her and the sexual tension between the two is out of this world HOT!<br><br><b>Hunter</b><br>I freaking loved Hunter! He is very ALPHA MALE, arrogant, possessive, protective, kinda scary, domineering, and can be surprisingly sweet at times. This is how I feel about Hunter...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392496ra/755565.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/679665.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Serena</b><br>Serena was an awesome heroine! She is smart, witty, has a backbone, and where Hunter is dominant, Serena is rebellious :) She is the perfect match for a guy like Hunter. <br><br>Jennifer Armentrout is very talented at creating humourous banter between her main characters and this book is no different!<br><br><b>"Please don't-" "Please don't what? Strangle the ever-loving common sense into you? I might do that."<br><br>*~*~*~*~*<br><br>"I can't get off? Oh, I most definitely can get off." </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423965ra/845034.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One aspect of this book that I thoroughly enjoyed is that this book is an adult novel, whereas the Lux books are young adult. The book is a lot steamier and doesn't gloss over the sexy scenes. <br><br>Overall, I enjoyed this book just as much as I enjoyed the Lux novels. I also refuse to pick a team (Arum or Luxen), I want to be on both LOL!<br><br><b>“You turn me on. You make me care about things I never cared about before. You make me think. You make me warm.”</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17948128087246591918" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Its was so <b>FUCKING</b> good, in every way. The characters are to die for, the plot really draws you in from start to finish, and lets not forget the steamy scenes that had me blushing and eyeing out my bookshelf *wink* and daydreaming my version of Hunter, a bookshelf, and me against it *sigh*.<br><br>Hunter has to be one of my most <b>FAVORITE</b> hunky, sexy, gorgeous, sarcastic and arrogant (bossy too) PNR hero's I've come across.<br><blockquote>

Seeing him open up and surprised by his feelings for the cute and feisty Serena was so loving and endearing to read about.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423707i/844333._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I LOVE, LOVE, LOVED this book and I'm hoping for more *fingers crossed* Arum in the near future.<br><br><b>This is a MUST read PNR lovers!!</b><br></span>

<div id="review_342275445" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/342275445" />
    <a title="Jana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4033116-jana"><img alt="Jana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590925674p2/4033116.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/342275445?book_show_action=true">Jun 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jana" href="/user/show/4033116-jana">Jana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4033116-jana?shelf=blog-reviewed">blog-reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4033116-jana?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4033116-jana?shelf=jennifer-l-armentrout">jennifer-l-armentrout</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4033116-jana?shelf=entangled">entangled</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4033116-jana?shelf=2013-reads">2013-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer342275445" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15431484913737292092">I know my review would never do this book justice but hey at least I tried, right? In case you're wondering, yes, the Queen of Everything Jennifer L. Armentrout has done it again. OBSESSION was everything I hoped for and more. I was dying for this book ever since she gave us some teasers last May and NOW I actually can't believe I've finally read it! <br/><br/>Hunter is definitely the baddest hot male character Jen has ever written. EVER. He's also my favourite which says a LOT. Sorry Daemon and Cam but H</span>
  <span id="freeText15431484913737292092" style="display:none">I know my review would never do this book justice but hey at least I tried, right? In case you're wondering, yes, the Queen of Everything Jennifer L. Armentrout has done it again. OBSESSION was everything I hoped for and more. I was dying for this book ever since she gave us some teasers last May and NOW I actually can't believe I've finally read it! <br /><br />Hunter is definitely the baddest hot male character Jen has ever written. EVER. He's also my favourite which says a LOT. Sorry Daemon and Cam but Hunter is definitely kicking both your asses. Hunter is not your typical hero. First, I doubt you'd even like him at the beginning. He's an ARUM - besides being one of the 'bad guys', he's also cold, an alpha male, has an ego the size of the planet and with such arrogance that will put Daemon to shame. But as you read on, you just can't help but really fall in love with him. I KNOW I DID. Like Serena says "You're more than a weapon, Hunter. So much more." There is so much more to him and by the end of the book, I'm oh so ready to marry and have his babies. YUM.<br /><br />If you love how feisty Alex and Katy are, then you'd adore Serena!! Serena made me laugh as much as Hunter did, and I love how big her heart is and how feisty she is with Hunter. She NEVER backs down from him and I just love their interactions. If you love Daemon and Kat's banter, you'd LOVE Hunter and Serena's. Made me laugh so much!<br /><br />You know what's so great about all this? Besides the sexy romance (which is my fav), there was this whole thing between the Luxen, Arum, the government and even humans. Those who've read the Lux series will obviously know more, but you can also read this as a stand-alone (she explains everything perfectly). And I really admire how Jen wrote this whole alien war thing being not just black and white. There's soooo many gray areas, and to be honest, there's NO good guy or bad guy. In the YA series, we get the Luxen point of view and we all deemed the Arum as the stupid ugly bad guys. But it's so far from that. I'm so thankful to JLA for writing this from the supposed enemy point of view. Arum can be just as interesting and good as the Luxen. I'm so not Team anybody. I love both the Luxens and Arums. :) <br /><br />If you thought that JLA couldn't write her books any more hotter, well then you're SO wrong. Hands down, OBSESSION is her hottest and sexiest book so far. I read a lot of adult/new adult smexy stuff, but some of the stuff here made me blush. The scenes are so beautifully written and not just there for the sake of it. (Definitely not for the younger readers but I am nearly an adult so :P)<br /><br />You're all probably so tired of me going on and on about Jen's fabulous writing, but I gotta say it again. She's one hell of a writer. Guys, she's one of the actual few who makes me WANT to lose sleep just because I HAVE to know what happens next. I started this in the late evening and didn't finish until the morning. (Which probably wasn't a good idea since I had a test in the morning but OH SO WORTH IT GUYS.) OBSESSION has a mix of everything you want: characters you can never get enough of, smexy romance with a touch of action and humour and basically just everything else ahhhhhh. GOSH IS IT SO OBVIOUS HOW MUCH I LOVE THIS BOOK? <br /><br />There's just so much I want to say about OBSESSION but I really can't so..*zips lips* But yes, some characters from the Lux YA series does make some appearances ;) And now I also kinda know why the fourth Lux book is called ORIGIN. *grin* This is so going on my favourites list and no doubt this will come up when I do my yearly Top 10 lists. My only wish is it: Can I have this on paperback please?? I NEED THIS ON MY SHELF. <br /><br />And...because I'm such a nice person, I'll end this review with one of my fav quotes from OBSESSION: <br /><br />""You're more than a weapon, Hunter. So much more."<br /><br />"With you? I am more, but not with anyone else. " <br /><br /><br /><br />So many hugs and thanks to the lovely people at Entangled - Liz Pelletier and Heather Riccio!! :D<br /><br />And of course to my fav author ever Jennifer L. Armentrout for being so awesome to her fans and for writing the best stories ever. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15431484913737292092" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer7741303961155476370">Audio – 3 stars <br/>Story – 3.5 stars<br/><br/>I enjoyed the first half of the book more than I did the second half. I really liked Hunter and Serena and their interactions had me chuckling often. Serena was feisty and kickass. Something I always appreciate in a heroine. I can’t stand a damsel in distress. After their initial meeting and having to go in hiding together, it seemed like not much else was happening until they had to go on the run again. I also had a problem with the time frame. That’s becoming m</span>
  <span id="freeText7741303961155476370" style="display:none">Audio – 3 stars <br />Story – 3.5 stars<br /><br />I enjoyed the first half of the book more than I did the second half. I really liked Hunter and Serena and their interactions had me chuckling often. Serena was feisty and kickass. Something I always appreciate in a heroine. I can’t stand a damsel in distress. After their initial meeting and having to go in hiding together, it seemed like not much else was happening until they had to go on the run again. I also had a problem with the time frame. That’s becoming more and more of an issue for me. I need more that a week to go by before the “L” word is introduced. Or for the story to be so engrossing that the time frame isn’t so obvious. The ending was also not satisfactory. It’s an HFN with an uncertain future of what’s to come. <br /></span>

<div id="review_611386686" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/611386686" />
    <a title="★★Sara Lizzy★★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17083195-sara-lizzy"><img alt="★★Sara Lizzy★★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1401476931p2/17083195.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/611386686?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="★★Sara Lizzy★★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="★★Sara Lizzy★★" href="/user/show/17083195-sara-lizzy">★★Sara Lizzy★★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17083195-sara-lizzy?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17083195-sara-lizzy?shelf=lux-series-and-arum-books">lux-series-and-arum-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17083195-sara-lizzy?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17083195-sara-lizzy?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer611386686" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2651747380895213573"><b>BR with Jo and Sammy 7/16/13-7/20/13</b><br/>(This was a re-read for me)<br/><br/>~~~~My Original review from 6/7/13~~~~<br/><b>5 STARS</b><br/><br/>Let me start by saying that if you haven't read <i>Opal</i> from the Lux series, I'd suggest <b>NOT</b> reading this book until you do. At about 83% into the book, even though names are not mentioned- Daemon makes an appearance and the cliffhanger in <i>Opal</i> is referenced.<br/><br/>I absolutely <b>LOVED</b> Hunter in this book, but you will <b>NEVER</b> hear me say anything remotely positive about any Arum when I'm reading a book</span>
  <span id="freeText2651747380895213573" style="display:none"><b>BR with Jo and Sammy 7/16/13-7/20/13</b><br />(This was a re-read for me)<br /><br />~~~~My Original review from 6/7/13~~~~<br /><b>5 STARS</b><br /><br />Let me start by saying that if you haven't read <i>Opal</i> from the Lux series, I'd suggest <b>NOT</b> reading this book until you do. At about 83% into the book, even though names are not mentioned- Daemon makes an appearance and the cliffhanger in <i>Opal</i> is referenced.<br /><br />I absolutely <b>LOVED</b> Hunter in this book, but you will <b>NEVER</b> hear me say anything remotely positive about any Arum when I'm reading a book in any <i>Lux</i> series- I already feel like I'm betraying Daemon by saying anything remotely positive about any Arum since they are the Luxen's mortal enemies LOL.<br /><br />This books begins where Serena's out with her friend Mel is talking about how she overhear the Senator Vanderson's sons arguing about something to do with how their father was going to ruin things with Daedalus and a Project Eagle and something to do with children in Pennsylvania. When their argument got heated, Mel said that they both lit up like a "glow worm". Because she was witness to this and the argument, when Serena and Mel leave the bar they are at, Serena witnesses a Luxen approach Mel's car and he blows it up, killing Mel in the process. Because Serena witnessed what happened- now the Senator has Luxen coming after her to kill her.<br /><br />This is how Hunter is introduced, he's at the airport- bound for the backwoods of West Virginia when he gets a call from Officer Zombro from DOD and is told that he needs to drop his plans and he will be watching over Serena since she has Luxen after her and it's his job to not only protect her, but find out how much she knows.<br /><br /><b>"During her police interview, Miss Cross relayed some information that the Daedalus is concerned about. Some key words that they are not familiar with."<br /><br />"She mentioned something about a Project Eagle. The Daedalus would like to know what this is"</b><br /><br />Hunter is not at all pleased about his assignment.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Sitting around, behaving, and being the Department of Defense's bitch was not in my nature.</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>I was not happy about this. There wasn't a patient bone in my body and the only reason I was ever around a woman was to sate a primal hunger. I didn't protect them. It wasn't in my nature, and the officers knew that. I wasn't the good guy here.<br /><br />There was a good chance I'd kill Miss Cross.</i>
</b><br /><br />Hunter and Serena were attracted to each other from the start.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>This man, with his deep voice and odd eyes, had to exude some kind of epic sex pheromones because I had a sudden image of us in a bed, our bodies twisting and rocking together.</i>
</b><br /><br />Part of the fun was that, while they had an attraction, they irritated each other and made each other angry and the banter between them was hilarious!<br /><br />After one of the times Hunter gave into temptation and fed on Serena, she was so pissed off that she started throwing things at him, and she was elbowing him also so Hunter ended up pinning her to the bed to get her to stop. <br /><br /><b>I couldn't move-couldn't breathe. Hunter weighed a ton, and every part of him that touched me was hard and cool. Heart racing into cardiac territory, I went completely still.<br />"Are you insane?" he growled. "Look at me!"<br />Shaking my head frantcally, I kept my eyes squeezed shut. "Please don't-"<br />"Please don't what? Strangle the ever-loving common sense into you? I might do that." There was a pause and his chest rose against mine. "Jesus H. Christ, woman, I didn't sign up for this. I think you gave me a flesh wound."<br />I pried open one eye, and then both. Those startling pale eyes, full of anger, fixed on mine.<br />"Are you done acting like a psychotic, cracked out Muppet baby?" he asked, and I could tell by the way his fingers spasmed around my wrists, he really wanted to shake. "Or do you need a couple more moments to return to sanity? I have all day. And you actually feel kind of good under me, so take your time."</b><br /><br />---------<br /><b>Good God, I wanted to hit him. "You <i>fed</i> off me, dude. I can't even categorize how messed up that is. That's <i>not</i> okay."<br />"I'll tell you what's not okay, is you throwing shit at me." Curiosity marked his expression. "Why did you throw something at me?" When I didn't answer, a muscle popped in his jaw. "You're not going to answer me? Or do I need to repeat myself for a third time? It's okay. I like to hear myself talk."<br />In a second, anger and irritation roared through me. Something about his cocky tone pissed me off. So did my body's reaction to him. Parts of me were all kinds of tingly, especially when I wiggled again and felt <i>him</i> twitch.<br />"Get off me." I tried to push him off, but that didn't work. "Get off me <i>now</i>!<br />"Or what?" He tilted his head down so that his mouth was inches from mine. "You going to pick up a picture frame next and wing it at my head?"<br />"Maybe," I snapped back.<br />"Then I can't let you up."<br />I stared at him in disbelief and sputtered, "You can't - Get off!"<br />One single brow arched up. "I can't get off? Oh, I most definitely <i>can</i> get off."<br />The flush increased until I felt like I was under the sweltering sun. Muscles in my stomach tightened. "That's not what I meant and you know it."<br />"Hmm, so you say....so you say"</b><br /><br />I'm not going to go into details of the whole story plot, as I don't want to give too much away, but I will say that as the attraction grows, Hunter gets more protective of Serena. He goes as far as killing Luxen and even killing the DOD agents that had originally assigned him to her when they had come to his house to kill her, to keep her safe. Hunter and Serena go on the run and he even removes and destroyed his opal anklet that has a tracker in it so the DOD can't track them. There's so much more to that story, but you'll just have to read the book to find out more.<br /><br />The chemistry between Serena and Hunter was explosive and the sex scenes in this book were more explicit than anything I've read in the Lux novels (not that I'm complaining). It was also interesting to hear from a Arum first hand what their lives are like and the different facts about the Luxen and Arum from an Arum's POV. In the Lux novels, you are led to believe that pretty much all Luxen are good and the Arum are all bad, but when you read this book, you realize that there is good and bad with both the Luxen and the Arum.<br /><br />I found it funny all the ways they described the Luxen throughout the book: Glow worm, light bulb, glowworm mafia of the universe, Glow sticks, Lite-Brite, guy who lit up like a Christmas tree, Rainbow Brite, glowbug, among many others.<br /><br />I loved how Hunter and Serena's relationship slowly progressed and they eventually fell in love with each other.<br /><br /><b>"Want to know a secret?"<br />"Depends."<br />He chuckled. "It's about the moment I knew I wanted you, that you'd be mine. That I'd fall in love with you."<br />Hearing him say that affected me deeply. It took a moment to speak. "When?"<br />"Sooner than you'd think."<br />"When?" I asked.<br />"The first day you were in my cabin. When you threw the statue at my head."</b><br />-------------<br /><br /><b>"You turn me on. You make me care about things I never cared about before. You make me think. You make me warm."</b> ~Hunter to Serena<br />-------------<br /><br /><b>
  <i>My future was one big fat unknown, but with Hunter by my side, I knew we'd make it. Things might not be orthodox or how I pictured spending my life, but I was alive and I was with someone I loved. However, I did know that things wouldn't be easy.<br /><br />My life was forever altered and would never, ever be the same. Maybe one day I could go back to a job like I had before. Maybe a million aliens would descend on Earth tomorrow. But right now? I had to live in the right now.</i>
</b><br /><br />If you have read <i>Opal</i> already, I highly recommend this book! It was fantastic!</span>
  <a data-text-id="2651747380895213573" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('oSI7BTw+nK2D69QJr/UA3hx7KZxU28AuJnHRRCj/B04BSwPQxmJAaLjQTppIlIe3c9H7nGFZ1D2KMxWMUYpm5Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AFySL0NlQqqFMpuSr0G/VWdJfWPku7HFxPUt+fQ2Zd+gNar6uTmeb74JAQFIIDg8COOvY9E5pdZot+kxjUMEdA==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer1808167173260847718">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br/><br/>To email me, please use the below addy. <br/>jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br/><br/># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors yo</span>
  <span id="freeText1808167173260847718" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>
